<div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;">
<span style="color: #666666; font-family: Arial; font-size: 13.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Courier;">This list is still incomplete! Who and Jungle People will be
doing double duty as fish, cadets, circus folk, courtroom folk, etc. and will
be on stage a lot. Being a member of a Who family doesn't sound too important
right now, but this really is a production that will have everyone involved in a
lot of action. </span></div>

<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%;">
<span style="font-family: Verdana;">Our
first meeting and rehearsal is <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Monday,
Jan. 14 at 3:30</b> in the auditorium.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;
</span>This includes all cast and crew!</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 200%;">
<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: Verdana;">Tuesday &#8211;</span></b><span style="font-family: Verdana;"> Full cast meet in the Choir Room at 3:30 for a
first music rehearsal!<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>After music
rehearsal, you will move to the auditorium for blocking.</span></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, May 16, 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kvUv51WJnoc/T7O_87ifv-I/AAAAAAAAAMI/oH2NjvRvrDI/s320/IMG_8436.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='107416652257263142' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='107416652257263142'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/05/dance-happening-thursday-may-17th-at.html'>A Dance Happening- Thursday, May 17th at 3:30</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-107416652257263142' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kvUv51WJnoc/T7O_87ifv-I/AAAAAAAAAMI/oH2NjvRvrDI/s1600/IMG_8436.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="247" kba="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kvUv51WJnoc/T7O_87ifv-I/AAAAAAAAAMI/oH2NjvRvrDI/s320/IMG_8436.JPG" width="320" /></a></div>
Please join RB's Repertory Dance Ensemble TOMORROW, May 17th at 3:30 in the RBHS Library as they present, "Tilted Silence."&nbsp; The dancers will perform a five minute dance using the aisles, bookshelves and tables of the Library as their performance stage.&nbsp; We hope to see you there.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TaA2ejXQloQ/T7O-r6XNwVI/AAAAAAAAAMA/VSVnq7DJrSg/s320/DSC_0215_2.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='2885504259910911467'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/05/congratulations-orchesis-dancers.html'>Congratulations Orchesis Dancers</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2885504259910911467' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Congratulations to the cast and crew of this year's Orchesis show, "Existence."&nbsp; Fifty-seven dancers graced the stage performing a variety of different dance styles and&nbsp;showcasing the versatility of the RBHS dancers.&nbsp; Student choreograpehrs included: Rachel Ackerman, Vilija Aleksa, Meredythe DiVittorio, Karen Fucinato, Sarah Jane Gembara,&nbsp;Nicole Kmet, Cassie Nakis, Jamie Payne, Alaina Sliz, Caroline Stanko and Danielle Ulloa.&nbsp; Guest Choreographers included professional artists Santo Scavuzzo III and Donnette Cannonie.<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TaA2ejXQloQ/T7O-r6XNwVI/AAAAAAAAAMA/VSVnq7DJrSg/s1600/DSC_0215_2.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="212" kba="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-TaA2ejXQloQ/T7O-r6XNwVI/AAAAAAAAAMA/VSVnq7DJrSg/s320/DSC_0215_2.JPG" width="320" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
Rachel Ackerman is pictured above in Vilija Aleksa' dance, "Everlasting,"&nbsp; To view more photos of this year's Orchesis show please visit <a href="http://rbhsfineartsdepartment.shutterfly.com/8100">http://rbhsfineartsdepartment.shutterfly.com/8100</a>.&nbsp; Also, a special thank you to Carla Novack for photographing the Orchesis show.&nbsp; To view Mrs. Novack's photos please contact her at 312-318-8779.&nbsp; The above photo is photographed by Ms. Novack.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7434208273318888855' itemprop='description articleBody'>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, March 14, 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9OufNXFcQQg/T2C1ZQ0qH8I/AAAAAAAAAL4/AUOGiJsYBZc/s320/IMG_7045.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5982909924677819882' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5982909924677819882'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/03/guest-choreographer-teaches-orchesis.html'>Guest Choreographer teaches Orchesis Dancers</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5982909924677819882' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9OufNXFcQQg/T2C1ZQ0qH8I/AAAAAAAAAL4/AUOGiJsYBZc/s1600/IMG_7045.JPG"><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 320px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 259px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5719770972377718722" border="0" alt="" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9OufNXFcQQg/T2C1ZQ0qH8I/AAAAAAAAAL4/AUOGiJsYBZc/s320/IMG_7045.JPG" /></a><br /><br /><br /><div>Currently, RB's Orchesis dancers are working with a professional dancer and choreographer. Mr. Santo Scavuzzo has performed for numerous dance companies and events including: Dance for Life, Same Planet Different World, Rodriquez Dance Theatre, and LehrerDance. In addition, Mr. Scavuzzo received his MFA in dance from the University of Iowa. RB dancers work hard learning new movements such as sudden knee drops, body layouts and quirky foot work. This dance, performed to Prince's Baby, I am a Star, will be performed as the opener to this year's Orchesis show on April 27th and April 28th. We hope you can make it.</div><br /><br /><br /><div>Save the Date- ORCHESIS DANCE CONCERT- Friday, April 27th &amp; Saturday, April 28th, RBHS Main Auditorium, 7PM</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fBcXoNLLFGU/T1Y3rDD5hKI/AAAAAAAAALs/eUgOzimXbz4/s320/IMG_6657.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/03/rbhs-dancers-qualify-for-state.html'>RBHS Dancers Qualify for State</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-774180147669814319' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fBcXoNLLFGU/T1Y3rDD5hKI/AAAAAAAAALs/eUgOzimXbz4/s1600/IMG_6657.JPG"><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 294px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 203px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5716817989688984738" border="0" alt="" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fBcXoNLLFGU/T1Y3rDD5hKI/AAAAAAAAALs/eUgOzimXbz4/s320/IMG_6657.JPG" /></a><br /><br /><div>Congratulations to the RBHS dancers for qualifying for state. The selected dance was choreographed by senior, Rachel Ackerman. It is a trio danced by senior dancer Jamie Payne, and junior dancers Alaina Sliz and Sarah Benya. The dance is titled "Keep me Quiet." Rachel was inspired by her having a secret. She says, "the dance is about having a really good secret and having to stay quiet- you can't tell anyone." The dance was proposed and choreographed as a part of Rachel's first semester final exam. The dance will be performed as a part of the student showcase on Saturday, May 19th at the Illinois H.S. State Dance Festival. Buffalo Grove H.S. will be hosting this year's festival.</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, February 29, 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dEyA2_5jLSU/T05S8I1Jz0I/AAAAAAAAATI/NPXWI7rHKjM/s320/IMG_6968.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2567806897243986616' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2567806897243986616'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/02/repertory-dancers-perform-at-hollywood.html'>Repertory Dancers Perform at Hollywood Elementary</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2567806897243986616' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dEyA2_5jLSU/T05S8I1Jz0I/AAAAAAAAATI/NPXWI7rHKjM/s1600/IMG_6968.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="209px" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dEyA2_5jLSU/T05S8I1Jz0I/AAAAAAAAATI/NPXWI7rHKjM/s320/IMG_6968.JPG" uda="true" width="320px" /></a></div><div style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none;">Every year RB's Repertory Dance Ensemble performs an educational art outreach performance&nbsp;for a&nbsp;local elementary school or organization.&nbsp; This year RBHS Repertory Dance Ensemble performed for the Hollywood Elementary School&nbsp;on Thursday, February 16, 2012.&nbsp; The dancers performed six dances and answered questions about dance, performing&nbsp;and choreography.&nbsp; Once the dancers were finished performing the fourth grade students broke into small groups and together&nbsp;they created a dance inspired by&nbsp;the Edgar Degas painting, Fin'd Arabesque; which&nbsp;both groups&nbsp;had been studying in class.<br />
<br />
To see more photos visit <a href="http://www.mysuburbanlife.com/photo_galleries/x1134098350/RB-dancers-visit-Hollywood">http://www.mysuburbanlife.com/photo_galleries/x1134098350/RB-dancers-visit-Hollywood</a></div><br />
<div class="separator" style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none; clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JtLp0t497I0/T05TUEPq7AI/AAAAAAAAATQ/7_DuHjkdWz0/s1600/IMG_7024.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; height: 192px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em; width: 286px;"><img border="0" height="212px" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JtLp0t497I0/T05TUEPq7AI/AAAAAAAAATQ/7_DuHjkdWz0/s320/IMG_7024.JPG" uda="true" width="320px" /></a></div><div style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-e5t6BKDlyms/T05SviuHPZI/AAAAAAAAATA/V-wkbGkFzv4/s1600/IMG_7021.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; height: 144px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em; width: 254px;"><img border="0" height="213px" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-e5t6BKDlyms/T05SviuHPZI/AAAAAAAAATA/V-wkbGkFzv4/s320/IMG_7021.JPG" uda="true" width="320px" /></a></div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, February 1, 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2899560688732861093' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2899560688732861093'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2012/02/music-update.html'>Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2899560688732861093' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dear Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
Congratulations to all our All State Musicians! This year every instrumentalist chosen to represent RB auditioned into the All State Honors Band. Molly Chaney was 2nd chair bass, Maddy Muntean was 9th chair first flute, Dovas Lietuvninkas was 2nd chair trumpet, and Andrew Payton was 4th chair tuba. Joining them in Peoria was Kyle Perfect and James Wang who each sang with the All State Honors Choir, and Haley Buntrock who received 3rd place for her composition &#8220;Falling.&#8221; Congratulations once again to all of you. Did you know that since 1991 RB has sent 51 musicians to the All State Festival?<br />
<br />
You can hear our all state musicians with their fellow colleagues on Thursday February 9th at 7:00 PM in the Auditorium. The band, directed by Kevin McOlgan, will be presenting their winter concert. <br />
<br />
A Quick look ahead: <br />
<br />
&#8226; February 17th, Jazz Ensemble hosts the Battle of the Big Bands. RB Auditorium, 7:00 PM, $10 adults, $5 students under 18 years old. <br />
<br />
&#8226; February 21st, Metro Suburban Band Festival (Only selectees) All Day<br />
<br />
&#8226; February 23rd, Winter Choir and Orchestra Concert. RB Auditorium, 7:00 PM, free admission<br />
<br />
&#8226; March 3rd, Solo and Ensemble Contest. Reavis High School, Burbank IL. All Day<br />
<br />
&#8226; March 5th, Chamber Orchestra Recital, 7:00 PM, Location TBA, free admission<br />
<br />
Now is the time to start thinking ahead towards summer music camps. If you are interested in attending one of the fabulous camps in the area and want more information, please speak to Mr. McOlgan or Mr. Baum. <br />
<br />
Did you know that the RB Music Department currently serves 248 students? That&#8217;s 17% of the entire school!<br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<br />
baumj@rbhs208.net Mcolgank@rbhs208.org

<div class='post-header'>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/10/choir-concert-tonight.html'>Choir Concert Tonight!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4079500672429099112' itemprop='description articleBody'>
The RB Choirs will present the first concert of the school year tonight at 7 p.m. in the RB auditorium.&nbsp; The Madrigal Singers, Chamber Choir, Concert Chorale and Treble/Bass Choir will perform pieces they have worked on since the beginning of this school year.<br />
<br />
In addition, Krisin Ripoli, Cynina Mason and Lex Richter will perform "Mama Who Bore Me" from the musical "Spring Awakening".&nbsp; <br />
<br />
This morning, the Choirs from S. E. Gross, Hauser and Komarek Schools will visit RB from 10:00 a.m. until 2:00 p.m.&nbsp; They will have the opportunity to sing with the RB choirs and see what we do in choir every day!&nbsp; We welcome all the Jr. High Students!<br />
<br />
Choir members are all working diligently on their IMEA music.&nbsp; Auditions are next Tuesday, October 11 at Carl Sandburg High School.&nbsp; Audition times will be posted today.&nbsp; All of the music students will take a bus to Sandburg together.&nbsp; Good luck on your auditions!

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, October 3, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8311279825578958297' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8311279825578958297'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/10/instrumental-music-update.html'>Instrumental Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8311279825578958297' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dear Instrumental Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
Thank you to the 35 band students who played for the Class of 1966 Reunion on Saturday, and the parents who helped with carpooling. Members of the class of 1966 have been raving about how great you sounded and how wonderful it was to have you at their reunion.<br />
<br />
Despite the poor weather, the band looked and sounded great! Our presence in the stands was excellent and the 8th graders really seemed to enjoy their time with us. Many thanks to the parents who helped buy and distribute the pizza and soda, as well as the parents who helped distribute water and set up the drum major podiums. <br />
<br />
IMEA Audition times have been posted. More information about when the bus will be leaving and returning will be made available shortly. Auditions will be held at Carl Sandburg High School on Tuesday, October 11th. <br />
<br />
A message from Lena regarding the Tour: the deadline for your trip deposit has been pushed back to October 17th. <br />
<br />
On November 5th, we will be hosting the IMEA Junior High Festival. We will have about 300 junior high students and their directors on campus that day. As such we will need everyone&#8217;s help the night before, and on that day to make everything run smoothly. Signups and more information will be made available shortly, however please mark your calendars now.<br />
<br />
This Thursday is the RB Orchestra Festival. We will be joined by 50 junior high students from Hauser to play music inspired by war. The concert will begin at 7:00 PM. Hope to see you there!<br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, September 6, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5893384573927859823' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5893384573927859823'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/09/instrumental-music-update.html'>Instrumental Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5893384573927859823' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Hello everyone! <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Sam Romo who purchased a vintage Buffet R13 Clarinet this weekend! It's always exciting when one of our students saves their own money to buy a professional instrument. Sam is a student of Colleen Corning, RB's clarinet teacher,&nbsp;who helped him find the right instrument.<br />
<br />
Also, Congratulations to Alex Buffo who had the opportunity to play&nbsp;Taps at Soldier's Field recently for the Illinois Warrior Summit.&nbsp;&nbsp;Alex played on stage&nbsp;beside country singer Rockie Lynne.&nbsp; Alex is part of the group "Buglers Across America" who provide buglers for different events, mostly funerals of veterans, and every once in a while something different and fun like this.<br />
<br />
This Saturday the Marching Band will be participating in the Von Steuben Day festival and parade. Come show your&nbsp;support for the band and love for all things German at our most memorable parade in the fall!<br />
<br />
IMEA&nbsp;auditions are fast approaching. If you need help of any sort please don't hesitate to see&nbsp;Mr. McOlgan or&nbsp;Mr. Baum.<br />
<br />
Sincerely, <br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<a href="mailto:baumj@rbhs208.org">baumj@rbhs208.org</a>&nbsp;<a href="mailto:mcolgank@rbhs208.org">mcolgank@rbhs208.org</a>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, August 23, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2907969354126793980' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2907969354126793980'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/08/instrumental-update.html'>Instrumental Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2907969354126793980' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: x-large;"><strong>RB Musicians shine outside the walls of RB!</strong></span></div><br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>Many Music students at RB choose to go to summer music camps around the world over the summer as a means of deepening their understanding of music. Here is just a sampling of what RB Musicians have accomplished this summer:<br />
<br />
<ul><li>&nbsp;Drum Major Vicki Curtin marched her way into the top 8 marchers at drum major camp during the final march off. </li>
<li>Anna Menendez won a scholarship. She was named Camper of the Week at Laurence University&#8217;s summer music camp. This honor grants Anna a scholarship to the camp next year, it also grants the same scholarship to another RB student! </li>
<li>Adrienne Witek Also attended Laurence University&#8217;s camp and was placed into the top Theory Class.</li>
<li>Mitchell Herman attended Oberlin&#8217;s summer music camp and studied electronic composition. </li>
<li>Lucia Mancini, Molly Chaney, and Kelly Haughland all attended the Blue Lake Fine Arts Camp.</li>
<li>Maurice Hubbard was chosen to play in this summer&#8217;s Rockford Youth Symphony. </li>
<li>Andrew Payton attended the Indiana University College Audition Prep. Camp and was named the top Tuba player at the camp.</li>
<li>Cassidy Fritsch attended a camp organized as a joint effort between Curtis Music Conservatory, Julliard, and the Manhattan School of Music. While there, Cassidy was named first chair oboe in the top band, and first chair Cor Anglais in the top orchestra.</li>
<li>Cathryn Cowell was chosen to represent America in the international Flaud Competition in Ireland. She competed among the world&#8217;s finest Irish fiddle players! </li>
</ul><br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>Congratulations and thank you for representing RB so well around the world. We are proud of all of you!<br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div><br />
<div>&nbsp;</div><br />
<div>&nbsp;</div><span style="font-size: large;"><strong>Instrumental Update:</strong></span><br />
<br />
The marching band practice that was scheduled for tonight has been canceled due to schedule conflicts. Next week&#8217;s practice has been moved to Wednesday to avoid the same schedule conflict. The practice will be from 6:00 PM until 8:00 PM. It is imperative that everyone be present at this practice as it&#8217;s our only practice since camp prior to our first game. <br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>The Honors Chamber Orchestra held its first practice of the year on Monday night. The group will be working on pieces by Haydn, Mozart, and Mahler to begin the year. <br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>Despite rain on the first day of marching band camp, this year&#8217;s camp was the most successful camp that we have had. The students learned 57 sets in two days and two hours! Be sure to come out on September 2nd to root on the band and check out all their hard work. Thank you to the music sponsors for providing the pizza party at the end of camp! Also thank you to all the mothers who are currently fitting the entire band for Marching Band uniforms, the band would not look as great as they do without your help. <br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div><br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>baumj@rbhs208.org mcolgank@rbhs208.org<br />
<br />
<div>&nbsp;</div>

          <div class="date-posts">

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/07/4th-of-july-marching-spectacular.html'>4th of July Marching spectacular!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2581477971287323427' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Hello,<br />
All those who are marching in the 4th of July parades should arrive to the band room by 7:45 AM so we can distribute T-shirts, warm up, and load the buses. A special thank you to the Brauer Family for letting us use their pickup truck to transport the low strings through the parade. also thank you to all the parents who have volunteered to help distribute water, and the Music Sponsors for supplying the water.<br />
<br />
We look forward to seeing those of you who cannot march with us along the parade route!<br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/environmental-dance-happening.html'>An Environmental Dance Happening</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1677950982987586065' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DFv5uMUXrqY/TdLXAvpfy1I/AAAAAAAAAIo/g_SK0F0qvQs/s1600/IMG_6062.JPG"><img style="float:left; margin:0 10px 10px 0;cursor:pointer; cursor:hand;width: 237px; height: 320px;" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DFv5uMUXrqY/TdLXAvpfy1I/AAAAAAAAAIo/g_SK0F0qvQs/s320/IMG_6062.JPG" border="0" alt=""id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5607780893820177234" /></a><br /><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_e4cifSBurc/TdLWt-YUlcI/AAAAAAAAAIg/K-vIIqcwIEc/s1600/IMG_6071.JPG"><img style="float:left; margin:0 10px 10px 0;cursor:pointer; cursor:hand;width: 320px; height: 251px;" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_e4cifSBurc/TdLWt-YUlcI/AAAAAAAAAIg/K-vIIqcwIEc/s320/IMG_6071.JPG" border="0" alt=""id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5607780571357156802" /></a><br />Inspired by the post-modern era of modern dance, Repertory Dance Ensemble choreographs an envrionmental piece on the front steps of the school.  Please join us on Thursday, May 26th at 3:30 to witness RB's very own Dance Happening! The raindate is Friday, May 27th at 3:30.

<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GrTPssuyHWI/TdaePhyGNKI/AAAAAAAAAI4/mgvD7b9B6yM/s320/IMG_6173.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/dancing-in-grant-park.html'>Dancing in Grant Park</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4544655463066513151' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GrTPssuyHWI/TdaePhyGNKI/AAAAAAAAAI4/mgvD7b9B6yM/s1600/IMG_6173.JPG"><img style="float:left; margin:0 10px 10px 0;cursor:pointer; cursor:hand;width: 320px; height: 240px;" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GrTPssuyHWI/TdaePhyGNKI/AAAAAAAAAI4/mgvD7b9B6yM/s320/IMG_6173.JPG" border="0" alt=""id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5608844375540249762" /></a><br />After attending the Alvin Ailey American Dance Theater performance twenty-two dancers headed over to Grant Park and Buckingham Fountain to play improvisation games and restage choreography inspired by the Alvin Ailey performance.  To see more photos visit the Fine Arts Department shutterfly account.

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, May 17, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fWbJdqBS_VE/TdLaOv7A5fI/AAAAAAAAAIw/awWbDNCSEXA/s320/IMG_4974.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='9024385869879685155' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='9024385869879685155'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/dancers-attend-alvin-ailey-american.html'>Dancers attend Alvin Ailey American Dance Theater performance</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-9024385869879685155' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fWbJdqBS_VE/TdLaOv7A5fI/AAAAAAAAAIw/awWbDNCSEXA/s1600/IMG_4974.JPG"><img style="float:left; margin:0 10px 10px 0;cursor:pointer; cursor:hand;width: 251px; height: 320px;" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fWbJdqBS_VE/TdLaOv7A5fI/AAAAAAAAAIw/awWbDNCSEXA/s320/IMG_4974.JPG" border="0" alt=""id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5607784432946701810" /></a><br />In honor of Alvin Ailey American Dance Theater celebrating it's 50th anniversary of Alvin Ailey's Revelations students studied the masterpiece in class.  On Thursday, May 19th twenty-two students will witness the grace, artistry and athleticisim as they attend a live performance of Alvin Ailey American Dance Theater performing Revelations at the Auditorium Theater in Chicago.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<a name='340235078811023894'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/choir-spring-concert.html'>Choir Spring Concert</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-340235078811023894' itemprop='description articleBody'>
The RBHS Choirs will present their Spring Concert on Tuesday, May 17 at 7:00 p.m. in the auditorium.&nbsp; Entitled, "The Show Must Go On!", the concert has a Broadway theme this year.&nbsp; Come enjoy music from "Hairspray", "Phantom of the Opera", "Mamma Mia!" and more.&nbsp; Many students will be featured in solos and ensembles.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/art-show-and-choir-concert-on-tuesday.html'>Art Show and Choir Concert on Tuesday 5/17</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6767540637875470537' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rKe9qYSffAs/Tc2ODnoNHmI/AAAAAAAAASg/G2Wgq7Svw8c/s1600/cat.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320px" j8="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rKe9qYSffAs/Tc2ODnoNHmI/AAAAAAAAASg/G2Wgq7Svw8c/s320/cat.jpg" width="312px" /></a></div>The annual Spring Art Exhibit will be displayed on Tuesday, May 17th.&nbsp; Please join us for a reception from 6-8p.&nbsp; The Viewer's Choice Award will be announced at 7:00p.&nbsp; Desserts will be provided by Mrs. Farlee's Family and Consumer Science Students.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
Come early for the art show and then head off to the Choir concert, "The Show Must Go On"<br />
<br />
Enjoy the RB Arts!

<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XhLaAFg-NIM/Tc1hA3kRa_I/AAAAAAAAASQ/CfTP9fBBaLc/s320/IMG_0789.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='196977246401253064'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/rb-orchestra-attendes-open-rehearsal-of.html'>RB Orchestra Attendes Open Rehearsal of the CSO With Yo Yo Ma!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-196977246401253064' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XhLaAFg-NIM/Tc1hA3kRa_I/AAAAAAAAASQ/CfTP9fBBaLc/s1600/IMG_0789.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240px" j8="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XhLaAFg-NIM/Tc1hA3kRa_I/AAAAAAAAASQ/CfTP9fBBaLc/s320/IMG_0789.JPG" width="320px" /></a></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">Yo Yo Ma and Stephen Lester play a duet for the audience prior to answering students' questions.</span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">On Thursday May 12th, RB Orchestra Students attended a field trip to hear Ricardo Mutti and Yo Yo Ma rehearse with the Chicago Symphony Orchestra at Symphony Center. Susan Synnestvedt, mother of Alex and Maddy Muntean, performs with the orchestra, it was nice to see a familiar face in the orchestra, RB students even applauded as she entered the stage! Students were delighted to hear Mason Bates&#8217; <em>The B Sides</em>, a modern piece that used electronic instruments and percussion effects to create dance club inspired classical music. Then Yo Yo Ma came out to rehearse the Schumann Cello Concerto. He played the piece entirely from memory flawlessly and with finesse and charisma that only a musician of the highest caliber can do. At times he would close his eyes and play with a sensitivity that won the hearts of the audience in a few notes, at other times he performed fiery bursts of notes, adding an exclamation point by jumping out of his seat. Needless to say, the RB students were amazed! The rehearsal concluded with the Strauss <em>Aus Italien</em>. Mutti&#8217;s carefully choreographed visualizations brought out the best of the orchestra, at times he even engaged the audience into the rehearsal. To cap off the afternoon, Yo Yo Ma and Stephen Lester led a Q&amp;A session with the audience. RB students Olivia Lauritsen and Findlay Ross both had the opportunity to have Yo Yo Ma answer their questions. </div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NgSGpmqxJcs/Tc1gtmO8eKI/AAAAAAAAASM/Cj5in_9Q2Ac/s1600/IMG_0795.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320px" j8="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NgSGpmqxJcs/Tc1gtmO8eKI/AAAAAAAAASM/Cj5in_9Q2Ac/s320/IMG_0795.JPG" width="240px" /></a></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">Olivia Lauritsen asks Yo Yo Ma and Stephen Lester when they decided to become a professional musicians.</span></div><br />
<br />
This was a great opportunity for the orchestra students of RB. We are very lucky to have one of the worlds best orchestras right here in Chicago! Everyone should take advantage of this world class institution, check out www.cso.org for tickets and program information. Also take a look at other photos from the trip on our pictures page.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, May 9, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2267638976972442324' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2267638976972442324'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/05/instrumental-music-update.html'>Instrumental Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2267638976972442324' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dear Instrumental Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
May is always an exciting month in the music department. On May 1st both the Jazz Band and the Jazz Ensemble played at This Must Be the Place in Lemont. Both groups played a high energy swinging sets to a packed room. The Jazz Band then went on to repeat their set at Hackneys of Palos Hills for yet another packed crowd and professional musicians on May 4th. Thank you to both venues for supporting music education and to Tom Fox and the Brass Tacks Big Band for featuring our students. <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Kevin Dinh and Ben Mitchell who have been selected to perform for Senior Awards Night this Wednesday along with Megan Welch and the Seniors of Madrigals. The evening will begin at 7:00 PM with pre-ceremony music provided by Sarah Otmanski and Maggie McLaughlin, and Mr. McOlgan. <br />
<br />
On Thursday the Orchestra will be going on a field trip to hear an open rehearsal of the Chicago Symphony Orchestra featuring Yo Yo Ma! <br />
<br />
All music ensembles will be photographed on the morning of May 19th. Students should arrive to school by 7:45 in their concert attire. The photo will be taken in the auditorium, more information about ordering this photo, or ordering photos taken earlier in the year will be made available at a later date. <br />
<br />
On May 21st the Jazz Band and Chamber Orchestra will be featured along with a Choir at the Riverside Arts Fair. The Jazz Band will begin at 2:00 PM and the Chamber Orchestra will begin at 2:45 PM. We hope to see many familiar faces in the crowd!<br />
<br />
On May 24th at 7:00 PM the Chamber Orchestra will hold its final recital of the year at Ascension Lutheran Church in Riverside. The group will be playing two contemporary pieces as well as the 4th movement from Tchaikovsky&#8217;s Serenade for Orchestra.<br />
<br />
The Apollo Awards will be held on May 26th, not May 19th as listed in the student handbook. This is an evening where we celebrate all of our musical accomplishments of the year and award our outstanding musicians. The evening starts at 7:00 PM in the main Gym, and is followed up with a reception to be held in the Cafeteria. <br />
<br />
Graduation will be held on June 3rd. All band students need to meet at 6:00 PM that evening dressed up. <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Kevin Dinh, Ben Mitchell, Sarah Otmanski, and Sam Romo who all played with the Protégé Philharmonic this weekend at Navy Pier. This is an outstanding orchestra featuring many of Chicago&#8217;s most talented young students. <br />
<br />
Please keep us informed of all your musical accomplishments! <br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<br />
baumj@rbhs208.org mcolgan@rbhs208.org

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/04/madrigal-singers-perform-im-yours.html'>Madrigal Singers perform "I'm Yours"</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, April 25, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pb-BsS5wtsw/TbcTadRXj8I/AAAAAAAAAIA/_ATfsc_yvsE/s320/POSTER%255B1%255D%255B1%255D.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/04/orchesis-dance-concert-this-weekend.html'>ORCHESIS DANCE CONCERT-THIS WEEKEND</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2987708511282445043' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pb-BsS5wtsw/TbcTadRXj8I/AAAAAAAAAIA/_ATfsc_yvsE/s1600/POSTER%255B1%255D%255B1%255D.JPG"><img style="display:block; margin:0px auto 10px; text-align:center;cursor:pointer; cursor:hand;width: 226px; height: 320px;" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pb-BsS5wtsw/TbcTadRXj8I/AAAAAAAAAIA/_ATfsc_yvsE/s320/POSTER%255B1%255D%255B1%255D.JPG" border="0" alt=""id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5599966006913503170" /></a><br />Join the RBHS Orchesis Dance Company this Friday, April 29th and Saturday, April 30th in the Main Auditorium at 7:00pm for a stellar performance of DANCE. Student choreographers include Rachel Ackerman, Vilija Aleksa, Brigitte Collazo, Meredythe DiViottorio, Louise Gangware, Sarah Jane Gembara, Allison Hornung, Hannah Langosch, Kayla Muldoon, Alaina Sliz, Caroline Stanko, Rima Lintikas AND GUEST HIP HOP CHOREOGRAPHER KATY KEMPEN. Tickets are 4.00 for students and seniors and 6.00 for adults. Children 6 and under are free.

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/04/instrumental-music-update_18.html'>Instrumental Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1644708836018112032' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Thank you to everyone who wrote such nice letters and emails in response to our Spring Concert last Thursday. The evening was splendid, and the kids sounded fantastic! Mr. McOlgan was especially moved by all the parents and students who took the time to meet his mother that night.<br />
<br />
<br />
Our field trip to see &#8220;Working&#8221; is Wednesday. Students will leave school 5th hour and should therefore be prepared to eat lunch at school. If you haven&#8217;t turned in your permission slips please turn it in A.S.A. P.<br />
<br />
The Apollo awards will be held on May 26th in the Main Gym and not on May 19th. Please adjust your calendars.<br />
<br />
Congratulations to Joe Wilkinson who played an outstanding audition at Elmhurst College. After the audition Joe was informed by the school that they really wanted him and are prepared to match any scholarship from another school. <br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<a href="mailto:baumj@rbhs208.org">baumj@rbhs208.org</a> <a href="mailto:McOlgank@rbhs208.org">McOlgank</a>@rbhs208.org

</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8742012815842318283' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none; clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xsokZGXO7Vk/TaTLCFJyyXI/AAAAAAAAAR0/4iC8hOj2s3M/s1600/471px-Sva_logo_stacked.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xsokZGXO7Vk/TaTLCFJyyXI/AAAAAAAAAR0/4iC8hOj2s3M/s320/471px-Sva_logo_stacked.jpg" width="249" /></a><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eKKKaUdAIWY/TaiYsZPrdNI/AAAAAAAAAR4/7gunD43dPdw/s1600/SamFrd+SVA+01.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="133" r6="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eKKKaUdAIWY/TaiYsZPrdNI/AAAAAAAAAR4/7gunD43dPdw/s200/SamFrd+SVA+01.jpg" width="200" /></a></div>Congratulations to Samantha Friend for being awarded a full-ride scholarship to&nbsp;participate in a three week art camp held at the&nbsp;School of Visual Arts in New York City.&nbsp; Sam&nbsp;received this award from the Scholastics&nbsp;Art and Writing organization.&nbsp; She qualified after receiving a&nbsp;Gold Award&nbsp;for her photograph at the Regional Scholastics Art Competition held in January.&nbsp; <br />
<br />

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, April 11, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='718210215601822766' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='718210215601822766'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/04/instrumental-music-update.html'>Instrumental Music Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-718210215601822766' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dear Instrumental Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
The Spring concert is upon us. Join us this Thursday evening at 7:00 in the auditorium. Students should be gathering their concert attire tonight to make sure they are ready for Thursday. The call time for students to arrive is 6:15. <br />
<br />
Thank you to all who attended Jazzapalozza V. It was a great evening of jazz featuring guest artist Sam Lauritsen. Sam is a RB graduate who performed on the very first Jazzapalozza and is now finishing his degree in Jazz Performance at Roosevelt University&#8217;s Chicago College of Performing Arts. Both RB Jazz groups sounded great. Thank you to everyone who brought treats to share, especially Mrs. Baum&#8217;s lemon squares. <br />
<br />
The Jazz Groups will be featured at This Must Be the Place on May 1st. The Jazz Ensemble will open the evening at 6:00 PM followed by the Jazz Band. Please call 630-243-1500 for reservations. <br />
<br />
The Jazz Band will open for the Brass Tracks Big Band at Hackneys in Palos Heights on May 4th. Their set will begin at 7:00. <br />
<br />
Mark your calendars for the Apollo Awards which will be held on May 19th at 7:00 PM. All music students will perform, and we will honor our outstanding students. <br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<br />
baumj@rbhs208.org mcolgank@rbhs208.org

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, March 25, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GURkH15UVls/TYy09Qsbf2I/AAAAAAAAAHo/W1EZpYhuJ7w/s320/IMG_5202.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='865074482602801229' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='865074482602801229'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/03/guest-hip-hop-choreographer-teaches-at.html'>Guest Hip Hop Choreographer teaches at RB</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-865074482602801229' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<blockquote></blockquote><blockquote></blockquote><p align="center"><span></span><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 237px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 170px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5588040202206281570" border="0" alt="" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GURkH15UVls/TYy09Qsbf2I/AAAAAAAAAHo/W1EZpYhuJ7w/s320/IMG_5202.JPG" /><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 243px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 165px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5588042668886993858" border="0" alt="" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HwahpMO0Jx0/TYy3M1y8K8I/AAAAAAAAAH4/sraUYXEEPyw/s320/IMG_5204.JPG" /></p><br /><div><div>The week of March 14th twenty-one Orchesis dancers worked with professional hip hop and contemporary dancer Katy Kempen. Recently, Katy toured with R. Kelly and Jay-Z where she performed with various award winning artists. Katy shared her stories of being a professional concert dancer and a dancer traveling on tours.  RB dancers can not wait to perform Katy's dance at this year's Orchesis show on April 29th and 30th. </div></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, March 22, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='7087051390794498078'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/03/choir-concert.html'>Choir Concert!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7087051390794498078' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Please come to a concert presented by the choirs of RBHS, Wednesday March 23 at 7:00 p.m. in the Auditorium.&nbsp; The concert will feature World Music, including "Jai Ho" from the movie "Slumdog Millionaire".&nbsp; We will also present the DVD the choirs made when they performed in Disney World.&nbsp; Hope to see you at the concert!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, March 21, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6837844701932971581' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6837844701932971581'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/03/instrumental-update.html'>Instrumental Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6837844701932971581' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dear Instrumental Music Community,<br />
<br />
Congratulations to everyone involved with the musical &#8220;The Wiz.&#8221; The pit sounded great, the crew performed amazingly, and the cast was exceptional. We hope you had the opportunity to <br />
<br />
<br />
&#8220;ease on down the road&#8221; to see the amazing work of the students in the music and drama departments.<br />
<br />
On March 5th many of our students participated in the IHSA Solo and Ensemble Contest. Between the choirs, bands, and orchestra students 162 Division 1 medals and 52 Division 2 medals were won. Great job Bulldogs! <br />
<br />
The Jazz Band will be performing at This Must Be the Place in Lemont on May 1st and at Hackneys May 4th. Please make reservations if you plan to attend the May 1st concert, we look forward to seeing you there!<br />
<br />
The Bands and Orchestras are busy working on their music for the spring concert. This year the concert will be on April 14th at 7:00 PM. <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Molly Chaney who has been accepted to Interlocken Music Festival this summer. <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Ben Mitchell and Sam Cox who just achieved the rank of Eagle Scout in troop 24. We are all very proud of you both!<br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, March 18, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-iqZoIsQbKA0/TYPh6Mk0eyI/AAAAAAAAARk/KilMbmmUs-Y/s320/IMG_0894.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/03/fine-arts-department-accepts-award.html'>Fine Arts Department Accepts Award</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-807662256915751697' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-iqZoIsQbKA0/TYPh6Mk0eyI/AAAAAAAAARk/KilMbmmUs-Y/s1600/IMG_0894.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" r6="true" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-iqZoIsQbKA0/TYPh6Mk0eyI/AAAAAAAAARk/KilMbmmUs-Y/s320/IMG_0894.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>&nbsp;<a href="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-rgpI7mzM6ZE/TYPh88-at9I/AAAAAAAAARo/UFb_g6Pyi2o/s1600/IMG_0891.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" r6="true" src="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-rgpI7mzM6ZE/TYPh88-at9I/AAAAAAAAARo/UFb_g6Pyi2o/s320/IMG_0891.jpg" width="240" /></a><br />
On Thursday, members of the Fine Arts department traveled to Springfield, Illinois to accept the Illinois Alliance for Arts Education School of Distinction Award.&nbsp; Mindy Haines also accepted the award for Dance Educator of the Year.&nbsp; Congratulations RB Fine Arts!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/03/art-students-metro-suburban-conference.html'>Art Students @ Metro Suburban Conference Event</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1272902341695097807' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none;"><a href="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-Jc0pBVrpd2s/TYNOAoWy6GI/AAAAAAAAARg/HeELeGhxE2s/s1600/IMG_2530.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" r6="true" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-Jc0pBVrpd2s/TYNOAoWy6GI/AAAAAAAAARg/HeELeGhxE2s/s320/IMG_2530.JPG" width="240" /></a>On Wednesday, 7 RBHS art students were selected to attend the Metro Suburban Conference Art Festival.&nbsp; Students displayed their artwork and attended workshops given by professional artists.&nbsp;&nbsp;Conference art teachers also met to collaborate on curriculum.&nbsp; <a href="https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-POYRB-aDGt8/TYNN_MyWSQI/AAAAAAAAARc/zk6-3V34aCs/s1600/IMG_2540.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" r6="true" src="https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-POYRB-aDGt8/TYNN_MyWSQI/AAAAAAAAARc/zk6-3V34aCs/s320/IMG_2540.JPG" width="320" /></a>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </div><div style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none;">Participating students included Paige Bottari, Krystyna Serhijchuk, Lila Hernandez, Olivia Lauritsen, Emily Kedzie, Dan Curtin, and Bailey Csech.&nbsp; </div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

Our annual AP Art Show will be exhibited at the Riverside Art Center.&nbsp; The opening&nbsp;reception is set for&nbsp;Friday, March 11th from 6:00-9:00pm.&nbsp; The artwork will remain on display through&nbsp;April 23rd.&nbsp;&nbsp;Featured artists include&nbsp;our current AP&nbsp;students and our 2011-12 AP&nbsp;students.&nbsp; See you there!<br />

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8MXOyTZn_hA/TWfnUDm8LcI/AAAAAAAAARE/_FU6MyQCS4k/s320/Epcot.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='9133142709724192658' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='9133142709724192658'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/rbhs-choirs.html'>RBHS Choirs</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-9133142709724192658' itemprop='description articleBody'>
We're back!&nbsp; Just think!&nbsp; At this time last week, we were running around Disney Hollywood in 80 degree weather!&nbsp; The choirs had a great time playing, working and performing in Disney World.&nbsp; They were attentive and enthusiastic about the workshop on Saturday morning.&nbsp; The performance at Downtown Disney on Sunday was very well attended.&nbsp; As people passed by, they stopped, and they STAYED for our performance.&nbsp; I think that says a lot about the students' singing.&nbsp; By the middle of the concert, all the seats were filled and there were 4 or 5 rows of people standing.&nbsp; Congratulations to the choir students!&nbsp; <br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8MXOyTZn_hA/TWfnUDm8LcI/AAAAAAAAARE/_FU6MyQCS4k/s1600/Epcot.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" l6="true" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8MXOyTZn_hA/TWfnUDm8LcI/AAAAAAAAARE/_FU6MyQCS4k/s320/Epcot.JPG" width="320" /></a></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-qboTnCYEEgI/TWfneAR-8UI/AAAAAAAAARI/zM55ELOoiTQ/s1600/Disney+Workshop.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" l6="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-qboTnCYEEgI/TWfneAR-8UI/AAAAAAAAARI/zM55ELOoiTQ/s320/Disney+Workshop.JPG" width="320" /></a></div><br />
Congratulations to Megan Welch!&nbsp; Megan&nbsp;won 1st place in the Tower Chorale Vocal Competition.&nbsp; She sang "I Don't Know How to Love Him" from "Jesus Christ, Superstar".&nbsp; Megan will receive a vocal scholarship and will perform on a concert with the Tower Chorale in May.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
We're looking forward to a very busy March.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
<div align="center"><span style="color: blue;">March 5 - IHSA Solo and Ensemble Contest</span></div><div align="center"><span style="color: blue;">March 18, 19, 20 - "The Wiz"</span></div><div align="center"><span style="color: blue;">Tickets are on sale in the business office!</span></div><div align="center"><span style="color: blue;">March 23 - Choir Concert</span></div><div align="center"><br />
</div><div align="center"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: center;">&#65279;Hope to see you at any or all of these events!</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, February 24, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6583606232764286964' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6583606232764286964'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/instrumental-update_24.html'>Instrumental Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6583606232764286964' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Hello Instrumental Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
The February concert season has come to an end. It&#8217;s a bit weird to not have a concert tonight after three Thursdays in a row with concerts. The first concert was the Battle of the Big Bands featuring the RB Jazz Ensemble, the second concert was the Winter Band Concert, and last week we closed out the season with the Winter Orchestra and Chamber Music Concert. All three concerts were spectacular! Thank you to everyone who came out to support our musicians. <br />
<br />
Permission slips have been distributed for Solo and Ensemble contest to be held on March 5th at Reavis High School. We just received the times today; students can look on the music office windows to find their times. <br />
<br />
Be sure to tune in to WFMT (98.7 FM) this Saturday at 10:00 AM for a live broadcast of the Merit School of Music Wind symphony featuring RB students Dovas Lietuvninkas, Adrienne Witek, and Andrew Payton. If you can&#8217;t listen at that time, the show will be repeated on March 3rd later in the evening. The program is called &#8220;Introductions&#8221; and features the talents of Chicago&#8217;s brightest young musicians.<br />
<br />
Connor Fagen, guitarist for Jazz Band recently performed for a full house at Fitzgerald&#8217;s Night club in Forrest Park. The club has recently begun a Sunday open teen mic. Marco Severini, Tyler Straka, and future RB Drummer Adrian Murphy performed last week at the night light in Berwyn. Thank you for representing RB with your talents!<br />
<br />
Please keep us up to date with all your accomplishments.<br />
<br />
Sincerely,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan

          <div class="date-posts">

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/enjoy-music-from-orchestra-concert.html'>Enjoy Music from the Orchestra Concert</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, February 17, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PowbsZcHbTc/TV08HEZ-LWI/AAAAAAAAARA/vp7pHPAMsIQ/s320/IMG_9001.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2602683723407915499' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2602683723407915499'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/art-student-wins-1st-place.html'>Art Student Wins 1st Place</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2602683723407915499' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PowbsZcHbTc/TV08HEZ-LWI/AAAAAAAAARA/vp7pHPAMsIQ/s1600/IMG_9001.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="254" j6="true" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PowbsZcHbTc/TV08HEZ-LWI/AAAAAAAAARA/vp7pHPAMsIQ/s320/IMG_9001.JPG" width="320" /></a></div>Congratulations to junior Maddie Muntean for receiving&nbsp;the&nbsp;Award for Excellence given by the West Suburban Artist Guild.&nbsp; Maddie's work&nbsp;earned 1st place out of 200 other pieces and has now been accepted into the Best of the Best art exhibit hosted by the Alliance of Fine Arts.&nbsp; Maddie was the only artist to receive this honor.&nbsp;&nbsp;Her painting&nbsp;titled 'Candied Sushi'&nbsp;will be on display at the Peabody Mansion in Oak Brook from March until May.&nbsp; Congratulations Maddie!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SpJde4kqTXo/TVVz-ex6AjI/AAAAAAAAAHg/7nPdNfK0kd4/s320/IMG_4769.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='7149552498788119308' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='7149552498788119308'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/dancers-perform-at-brook-park.html'>Dancers Perform at Brook Park Elementary</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7149552498788119308' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SpJde4kqTXo/TVVz-ex6AjI/AAAAAAAAAHg/7nPdNfK0kd4/s1600/IMG_4769.JPG"><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 303px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 217px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5572487631192326706" border="0" alt="" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SpJde4kqTXo/TVVz-ex6AjI/AAAAAAAAAHg/7nPdNfK0kd4/s320/IMG_4769.JPG" /></a><br /><div>On Thursday, February 10th Repertory Dance Ensemble performed an educational art outreach program for 115 4th graders at Brook Park Elementary School. The dancers performed a variety of different dance styles while teaching about the art of dance. The program also included audience participation and one lucky Brook Park student by the name of Ashley was chosen to choreograph on the RB dancers. Congratulations, Ashley.<br /></div><div>Lastly, a special thank you to Brook Park teacher Joanne Janetopoulos for inviting RB to perform for her students. It was a wonderful day.</div><br /><div>To see more photos of the performance please visit <a href="http://rbhsfineartsdepartment.shutterfly.com/697">http://rbhsfineartsdepartment.shutterfly.com/697</a></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/visitors-to-choir-room.html'>Visitors to the Choir Room</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-420322905344299543' itemprop='description articleBody'>
The Madrigals enjoyed a recent performance of "No Comment", an a cappella group from the University of Illinois.&nbsp; The group&nbsp;entertained us with a great concert, including&nbsp;a medley from the musical "Spring Awakening", "Shark in the Water" and covers of other popular songs.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
Concert Chorale is learning a folk song from Poland - in Polish, of course!&nbsp; Stephanie Olszewski's grandmother has been kind enough to come to our classroom twice this week to tutor all of us in Polish diction.&nbsp; It isn't easy!&nbsp; But we think it will all be worth it in the end.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
How many days until we leave for Disney World? <span style="font-size: x-large;">9!!!</span> But who's counting?&nbsp; Seventy seven people that I know of....&nbsp; <br />
<br />
If you're in Florida that weekend, come hear the choirs on Sunday, Feb. 20 at 5:45 p.m. at the Water Side Stage in Downtown Disney.&nbsp; On Saturday, the choirs will also participate in a Disney Sings workshop.&nbsp; <br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><br />
</div><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ORgTi47ArmE/TVQsMEIBYTI/AAAAAAAAAQ4/BK1J0tTHXK4/s1600/2011-02-07+09.30.31.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" h5="true" height="240" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ORgTi47ArmE/TVQsMEIBYTI/AAAAAAAAAQ4/BK1J0tTHXK4/s320/2011-02-07+09.30.31.jpg" width="320" /></a></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KbCI66iJry0/TVQr0XDbmVI/AAAAAAAAAQ0/l95K2xnLNu0/s1600/2011-01-13+14.24.26.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" h5="true" height="240" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-KbCI66iJry0/TVQr0XDbmVI/AAAAAAAAAQ0/l95K2xnLNu0/s320/2011-01-13+14.24.26.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, February 8, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='7747620027872392822' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='848305301518442136' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='848305301518442136'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/instrumental-update.html'>Instrumental Update</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-848305301518442136' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Hello Music Community,<br />
<br />
<br />
Thank you to everyone who came out in support of the Jazz Ensemble last Thursday evening. The band sounded great and warmed the crowd up for the two outstanding pro bands to follow! <br />
<br />
The Annual Winter Band concert will be held this Thursday, February 10 at 7:00 PM in the auditorium. Highlights include Ben Mitchell performing the Straus French horn Concerto, Prokofiev&#8217;s classic <em>Peter and the Wolf</em> acted out by RB&#8217;s own Shenanigans, and a setting of <em>My Lord What a Morning</em> in honor of Black History Month. <br />
<br />
Congratulations to Marco Severini, Tyler Straka, and Adrian Murphy who performed at Brixies in Brookfield for the annual Special Olympics fundraiser. It&#8217;s great to volunteer for such a noble cause, they sounded great! <br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
See you Thursday,<br />
<br />
Mr. Baum and Mr. McOlgan<br />
<br />
baumj@rbhs208.org Mcolgank@rbhs208.org

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/art-students-use-unique-model.html'>Art Students use a Unique Model</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8513899711570650093' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxiajJrJHI/AAAAAAAAAQo/t5a5F_PHdwY/s1600/dog1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" h5="true" height="150" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxiajJrJHI/AAAAAAAAAQo/t5a5F_PHdwY/s200/dog1.JPG" width="200" /></a></div>Drawing II students experienced an unexpected visitor as their model for the day.&nbsp; Yogi, Mrs. Mortensen's newfoundland, posed for the class as the artists&nbsp;worked to develop the form using a variety of mediums.&nbsp; <br />
<br />
Thanks Yogi!&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="border-bottom: medium none; border-left: medium none; border-right: medium none; border-top: medium none; clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxiegySnwI/AAAAAAAAAQs/vRqG9QJwqSU/s1600/drawing+dog.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; cssfloat: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" h5="true" height="150" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxiegySnwI/AAAAAAAAAQs/vRqG9QJwqSU/s200/drawing+dog.JPG" width="200" /></a></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<a name='4217059326247954967'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/shennanigans-on-tv.html'>Shennanigan's on TV!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4217059326247954967' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxgaH127CI/AAAAAAAAAQk/vSYNWJnY3Ic/s1600/scan0002.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" h5="true" height="200" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUxgaH127CI/AAAAAAAAAQk/vSYNWJnY3Ic/s200/scan0002.jpg" width="150" /></a></div>Shennanigan's most recent show, "Welcome to my Tollbooth" is available on RBTV this weekend.&nbsp; Viewers can watch at 9:05pm on Friday, Saturday, and Sunday evening.&nbsp; Just turn on Comcast channel 16, AT&amp;T U-Verse 99,&nbsp;or&nbsp;watch at&nbsp;<a href="http://www.rbtv.tv/">http://www.rbtv.tv/</a>&nbsp;&nbsp; Enjoy!<br />
<br />
Performers include Drew Kohler, Jacob Palka, Nick Rauba, Paul Landahl, Sara Nie, Andrew Brondos, George Suchy, Sam Friend, Marty Gross, Allison Nicolai, Abraham Ourth, Erik Kramer, and James Landahl
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, February 3, 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUrXMFkyVpI/AAAAAAAAAQc/FfSIyeuHJGE/s320/IMG_9001.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>

<a name='188343905404991076'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://rbfinearts.blogspot.com/2011/02/art-students-win-awards-at-triton-cc.html'>Art Students Win Awards at Triton CC Competition!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-188343905404991076' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUrXMFkyVpI/AAAAAAAAAQc/FfSIyeuHJGE/s1600/IMG_9001.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="252" s5="true" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUrXMFkyVpI/AAAAAAAAAQc/FfSIyeuHJGE/s320/IMG_9001.JPG" width="320" /></a></div>Congratulations to the following art students for their recent success at the Triton Community College art competition.<br />
<br />
<u>Best Painting Award</u>: Maddie Muntean<br />
<br />
<u>Blue Ribbon Award:</u> <br />
Elise Castelaz (Computer Art)<br />
Deanasia Sanders (Photo)<br />
SarahJane Gembara (Drawing)<br />
<br />
<u>Red Ribbon Award:</u><br />
Ercolani Chiara (Ceramics)<br />
Kiley Rusen (Computer Art)<br />
Andrew Scafidi (Photo)<br />
Hannah Soppo (Photo)<br />
Jessica Huebner (Drawing)<br />
Paige Bottari (Painting)<br />
Salem Baer (Painting)<br />
Kaite Wallner (Ceramics)<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUrXpaUib7I/AAAAAAAAAQg/R07zc4Bx9ss/s1600/IMG_9029.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; cssfloat: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="234" s5="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_dUDXWouB7hU/TUrXpaUib7I/AAAAAAAAAQg/R07zc4Bx9ss/s320/IMG_9029.JPG" width="320" /></a></div><br />
<u>Yellow Ribbon Award:</u><br />
Tatiana Aerozaga (Photo)<br />
Isabella Soluri (Photo)<br />
Lonely Bridge (Photo)<br />
Ricardo Herrera (Drawing)<br />
Anne Sventy (Painting)<br />
Colin Roberts (Painting)<br />
Jenn Grasser (Painting)<br />
Amanda Biro (Ceramics)<br />
Jon Schereck (Ceramics)<br />
Allison Taber (Ceramics)<br />
Michael Zeman (Ceramics)<br />
Tyler Siebert (Ceramics)<br />
Luis Gonzalez (Ceramics)<br />
Erin McKenna (Ceramics)<br />
Selsa Carmona (Sculpture)
